# 9.8.2 Thermal Registers

@{Key=9.8.2; Title=Thermal Registers; Body=Refer to "Reading Register Tables" in the Introduction chapter for the register table protocol as well as recommendations for accessing registers. All SOC_THERM registers are in the APB address space. Refer to the Address Map section for the base addresses.
#### 9.8.2.1 Thermal Sensor Registers
- SOC_THERM_TSENSOR_TJ_MAX_0
- Offset: 0x8
- Read/Write: RO
- Parity Protection: N
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xx00,0000,0000,0000,0xxx)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0
- TJ_MAX_VLD
16:3 0x0
- TJ_MAX_TEMP

- SOC_THERM_EDP_OC_ALARM_OC1_CFG_0
- Offset: 0x4810
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: N
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000004 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,0000,0100)

- Thermal Registers
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 MASK:
- Used to mask the oc_alarm input. MASK=1=> OC1_alarm input is forced to
1. MASK=0=> OC_alarm input = the value on the pin 0 = DISABLE 1 = ENABLE 0x0 LONG_LATENCY_THROTTLE:
- Used to inform the CAR PLLx Hardware Controller that Hardware is
expected to control the PLL for large amounts of time when this OC alarm is engaged 0x0 HW_RESTORE_EN:
- Auto-restore system to un-throttled state after this alarm is de-asserted
0 = DISABLE 1 = ENABLE 0x0 PWRGOOD_MASK: Mask the throttling if power is not good. 0 = ENABLE_THROTTLE 1 = DISABLE_THROTTLE 3:2 0x1 THROTTLE_MODE:
- To select sticky Vs brief mode throttling
0 = DISABLED 1 = STICKY 2 = BRIEF 3 = RESERVED 0x0 ALARM_POLARITY: 1: assert low, 0: assert high 0x0 EN_THROTTLE:
- Enable the throttling on this overcurrent alarm
- SOC_THERM_EDP_OC_ALARM_OC1_CNT_THRESHOLD_0
- Offset: 0x4814
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: N
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0b0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
31:0 0x0 EVENT_CNT_THRESHOLD:
- Event count threshold to raise interrupt, 0-rise interrupt for every
event

- Increments for every oc_event. Cleared when interrupt is cleared

- Thermal Registers
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000004 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,0000,0100)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 MASK:
- Used to mask the oc_alarm input. MASK=1=> OC1_alarm input is forced to
1. MASK=0=> OC_alarm input = the value on the pin 0 = DISABLE 1 = ENABLE 0x0 LONG_LATENCY_THROTTLE:
- Used to inform the CAR PLLx Hardware Controller that HW is expected to
control the PLL for large amounts of time when this OC alarm is engaged 0x0 HW_RESTORE_EN:
- Auto-restore system to un-throttled state after this alarm is de-asserted
0 = DISABLE 1 = ENABLE 0x0 PWRGOOD_MASK: Mask the throttling if power is not good. 0 = ENABLE_THROTTLE 1 = DISABLE_THROTTLE 3:2 0x1 THROTTLE_MODE:
- To select sticky Vs brief mode throttling
0 = DISABLED 1 = STICKY 2 = BRIEF 3 = RESERVED 0x0 ALARM_POLARITY: 1: assert low, 0: assert high 0x0 EN_THROTTLE:
- Enable the throttling on this overcurrent alarm

- Bit
- Reset
- Description
31:1 0x7fffffff EVENT_DUR_THRESHOLD:
- An interrupt is triggered when TOTAL_EVENT_DUR >=
EVENT_DUR_THRESHOLD.
- To deal without counter rollovers, EVENT_DUR_THRESHOLD is
treated as always being within -2^(bitwidth-1) to +2^(bitwidth-1) of TOTAL_EVENT_DUR 0x0 LAST_MSB:
- Software should write the MSB of TOTAL_EVENT_DUR to this
register after every read. This enables OVERFLOW to detect overflows

- SOC_THERM_EDP_OC_ALARM_OC1_CFG_0
- Offset: 0x4810
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: N
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000004 (0bxxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,xxxx,0000,0100)

- Thermal Registers
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 MASK:
- Used to mask the oc_alarm input. MASK=1=> OC1_alarm input is forced to
1. MASK=0=> OC_alarm input = the value on the pin 0 = DISABLE 1 = ENABLE 0x0 LONG_LATENCY_THROTTLE:
- Used to inform the CAR PLLx Hardware Controller that Hardware is
expected to control the PLL for large amounts of time when this OC alarm is engaged 0x0 HW_RESTORE_EN:
- Auto-restore system to un-throttled state after this alarm is de-asserted
0 = DISABLE 1 = ENABLE 0x0 PWRGOOD_MASK: Mask the throttling if power is not good. 0 = ENABLE_THROTTLE 1 = DISABLE_THROTTLE 3:2 0x1 THROTTLE_MODE:
- To select sticky Vs brief mode throttling
0 = DISABLED 1 = STICKY 2 = BRIEF 3 = RESERVED 0x0 ALARM_POLARITY: 1: assert low, 0: assert high 0x0 EN_THROTTLE:
- Enable the throttling on this overcurrent alarm
- SOC_THERM_EDP_OC_ALARM_OC1_CNT_THRESHOLD_0
- Offset: 0x4814
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: N
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0x00000000 (0b0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000,0000)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
31:0 0x0 EVENT_CNT_THRESHOLD:
- Event count threshold to raise interrupt, 0-rise interrupt for every
event

1. MASK=0=> OC_alarm input = the value on the pin 0 = DISABLE 1 = ENABLE 0x0 LONG_LATENCY_THROTTLE:
- Used to inform the CAR PLLx Hardware Controller that HW is expected to
control the PLL for large amounts of time when this OC alarm is engaged 0x0 HW_RESTORE_EN:
- Auto-restore system to un-throttled state after this alarm is de-asserted
0 = DISABLE 1 = ENABLE 0x0 PWRGOOD_MASK: Mask the throttling if power is not good. 0 = ENABLE_THROTTLE 1 = DISABLE_THROTTLE 3:2 0x1 THROTTLE_MODE:

0 = DISABLED 1 = STICKY 2 = BRIEF 3 = RESERVED 0x0 ALARM_POLARITY: 1: assert low, 0: assert high 0x0 EN_THROTTLE:

- Bit
- Reset
- Description
0x0 MASK:
- Used to mask the oc_alarm input. MASK=1=> OC1_alarm input is forced to
1. MASK=0=> OC_alarm input = the value on the pin 0 = DISABLE 1 = ENABLE 0x0 LONG_LATENCY_THROTTLE:
- Used to inform the CAR PLLx Hardware Controller that Hardware is
expected to control the PLL for large amounts of time when this OC alarm is engaged 0x0 HW_RESTORE_EN:
- Auto-restore system to un-throttled state after this alarm is de-asserted
0 = DISABLE 1 = ENABLE 0x0 PWRGOOD_MASK: Mask the throttling if power is not good. 0 = ENABLE_THROTTLE 1 = DISABLE_THROTTLE 3:2 0x1 THROTTLE_MODE:
- To select sticky Vs brief mode throttling
0 = DISABLED 1 = STICKY 2 = BRIEF 3 = RESERVED 0x0 ALARM_POLARITY: 1: assert low, 0: assert high 0x0 EN_THROTTLE:
- Enable the throttling on this overcurrent alarm

31:1 0x0 TOTAL_EVENT_DUR:

== 1 or TOTAL_EVENT_DUR[31] 1->0 && LAST_MSB == 0
- SOC_THERM_EDP_OC_MON_ALARM_OC1_DUR_THRESHOLD2_0
- Offset: 0x4b14
- Read/Write: R/W
- Parity Protection: N
- Shadow: N
- SCR Protection: 0
- Reset: 0xfffffffe (0b1111,1111,1111,1111,1111,1111,1111,1110)
- Bit
- Reset
- Description
31:1 0x7fffffff EVENT_DUR_THRESHOLD:
- An interrupt is triggered when TOTAL_EVENT_DUR >=
EVENT_DUR_THRESHOLD.
- To deal without counter rollovers, EVENT_DUR_THRESHOLD is
treated as always being within -2^(bitwidth-1) to +2^(bitwidth-1) of TOTAL_EVENT_DUR 0x0 LAST_MSB:
- Software should write the MSB of TOTAL_EVENT_DUR to this
register after every read. This enables OVERFLOW to detect overflows

## 9.9 In-System Test Controller (IST)}.Body)
